 jammu-kashmir main pharma udyog kaa bazaar kareeb 1,200 se 1400 karod rupee kaa he
 In comparison, markets like Maharashtra and UP are around 20 times more
 jammu dawa udyog kaa pramukh centre he or yahaan lupin, san pharma, cadila pharmaceuticals jaisi kai companiyon ke kaarkaane hai
 There are a total of 50 such factories in Jammu, some of which are also local manufacturers
 jammu-kashmir main kaaphi sasti he bijaliaaj jab desh ke zyaadaatar sthanon par jal sankat chal rahaa he or bijli kii laagat badhati ja rahi he, jammu-kashmir is maamle main kaaphi behatar he
 Electricity is available in Jammu at around Rs 2 per unit, while in other areas of the country electricity is available at Rs 6 to 7 per unit
